  <script data-hook="s-pre-opti" data-react-helmet="true">
   (function(window) {
var getCookie = function (name) {
  var value = "; " + document.cookie,
      parts = value.split("; " + name + "=");
  if (parts.length == 2) return parts.pop().split(";").shift();
};
function getUrlParameter(name) {
  name = name.replace(/[\[]/, '\[').replace(/[\\]]/, '\\]');
  var regex = new RegExp('[\\?&]' + name + '=([^&#]*)');
  var results = regex.exec(window.location.search);
  return results === null ? '' : decodeURIComponent(results[1].replace(/\+/g, ' '));
};

var localStorageUserContext = localStorage.getItem('__uc'),
    userContext = localStorageUserContext && JSON.parse(localStorageUserContext),
    userSegment = 'Unknown',
    userlevel,
    currentPlan,
    demographics,
    segment,
    businessType,
    userType,
    sysfig,
    sysfigUserLevel,
    utmMedium;

if (userContext) {
  demographics = userContext.demographics;
  businessType = demographics && demographics.business_type;
  userType = demographics && demographics.user_type;


  switch (userType) {
    case 'consumer':
      segment = 'personal';
      break;
    case 'business':
      if (businessType && businessType !== 'other') {
        segment = businessType;
      } else {
        segment = 'business';
      }
      break;
    case 'other':
      segment = 'other';
      break;
    default:
      segment = '';
  }
  segment = segment.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + segment.slice(1);

  userlevel = userContext.currentPlan;
  userSegment = segment;
} else {
  try {
    sysfig = getCookie('sysfig');
    sysfigUserLevel = sysfig && JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(sysfig)).user;
  } catch (error) {
    sysfigUserLevel = null;
  }
  userlevel = sysfigUserLevel || 'visitor';
}

utmMedium = getUrlParameter('utm_medium');
if (utmMedium && utmMedium === 'email' && userlevel === 'visitor') {
  userlevel = 'from_email';
}

window.optimizely = window.optimizely || [];
window.optimizely.push({
  type         : 'cookieDomain',
  cookieDomain : window.location.host
});

const userAttributes = {
  customer_type : userlevel,
  user_segment  : userSegment
};

window.optimizely.push({
  type       : 'user',
  attributes : userAttributes
});

window.optimizelySettings = window.optimizelySettings || {};
})(window);
  </script>
